This is the logial foundation for for Relativity Theory, Probability Theory, and for

Quantum Theory. Contents is the following:

1 Introdution. 2 Classial logi. 3 Time and spae. 3.1 Reorders. 3.2 Time. 3.3

Spae. 3.4 Relativity. 4. Probability. 4.1 Â-funtions. 4.2 Independent tests. 4.3

Funtion of probability. 4.4 Conditional probability. 4.5 Classial probability 4.6 B-

funtions and lassial propositional logi. 4.7 Consisteny of the probability funtion.

4.7.1 Nonstandard numbers. 4.7.2 Model. 5. Quantum theory. 5.1 Events and the

moving equations. 5.2 Rotations of the x5Ox4 system and Â-bosonn. 5.3 Masses. 5.4

The one-mass states, partiles and antipartiles. 5.5 The two-masses states. 5.5.1 Neu-

trinno. 5.5.2 Eletroweak transformations. 5.6 Rotations of the Cartesian oordinates

system and quarrks. 5.7 Gustatory pentads. 5.8 Two events. 5.9 The dimension of

physial spae. 5.10 The events- probability interpretation of Quantum Theory. 6.

Conlusion.
